< Review>
Disappointing to say the least. I've been here twice, just to give a fair chance. Both times were lacking. The first time i got the top tier pedicure and acrylic fill with gel overlay.
My pedicure was super fast, and I don't think i would even call what i received a massage. She basically tickled my legs.
My fill wasn't too bad m, but it wasn't what i wanted. She did change the shape of my nails and took out the arch that was there.
The second time I received a fill- acrylic with gel overlay, and it was awful. The gal didn't take off all the old color before she applied the acrylic even when I asked her 3 times to get it off.
She changed the shape of every nail and they are not the same. Some are squaval, some are round. She did a repair and didn't shape it well at all, bot only is it square it's a big hump of acrylic that looks ridiculous. The gel color doesn't even coat the whole nail and there is such a huge definition between my acrylic and cuticle it looks like it wasn't smoothed out and I need a fill already.
The staff is not the friendliest either. When I arrived, a man asked me "What do you want?"  They often carry on in their own conversations and seem to pay little interest in client expectations for services entail.
I won't be going back.</Review>

<Text>When you need something right away and the closet store is Walmart, it became a life saver for me. I was eating some Carne asada tacos at work and I got a piece of meat stuck between my teeth. < Text>
Today was my worst experience at Walmart ever! They are supposed to be so great for pricing and price matching, but they are not. I was buying some tie downs and in the isle found 4 for the price of $9.44. Such a deal! I was so excited!! They had all of the 4 packs for this price. We grabbed 3, only to get to the register and be told they are actually $15.44 each. I had them go and price check, because why would all of the same 4 packs be under the $9.44 price if they were not that price. I understand then being in the wrong spot, or if only one or a few were. They were not, they messed the price tags up and then would only give me the $9.44 for 1 of the 3 I was purchasing. < Text>
Auto service at this location is a mess. They've got no idea how long a job will take and no idea how to do it right.  Went in to get a battery changed....and added an oil change to service order.

1)  I knew that I needed a battery.  (AAA had tested it when they came out to start the car), nonetheless, the girl on the counter insisted she would not sell me one until her mechanic tested it.  Apparently my service time was extended because the shop didn't know which battery to install....so they just waited for the sales staff..   I had to intervene and tell the sales help to send the battery I wanted out to the service floor.

2) Pushed to up-sell an air filter...told her no that I had changed it only a few months ago.  Seemed unwilling to take no for an answer.

3)  When I received my car back (1.5 hours, not the 45 I was promised), it was hard to start and idled rough regularly missing cylinders. On opening the hood, *both* battery cables were loose, and only finger tight.  Had to hunt down the mechanic to remedy this...all the while insisting that it wasn't *his* fault.  (seriously?  He's the one who changed the battery)

4)  Got about 1 mile away from the store when the check engine and other trouble lights came on.  Was already late for an appointment, so I did not return to Walmart.  The next morning I took the car to a local auto parts store.to borrow an OBD II reader to read the trouble codes. Came up with "engine too lean" & "mass flow air problem."  Eventually sorted this out with another trip under the hood.  Despite telling the auto center staff I did not want or need an air filter, they'd obviously checked it anyway...
....because one of the filter box latches was left undone, and the hose from the crankcase to the air system was hanging disconnected (one needs to disconnect this to get the filter box lid off.)  It certainly was not that way when it arrived at Walmart.

5)  Like another person on this thread had mentioned, apparently Walmart''s mechanics can't be bothered to reset the "service needed" light.  Lazy and/or sloppy.

Do yourself a favor....   The pennies you save by taking it here will be repaid in all sorts of wasted time, and having to get others to do the jobs right.</Text>
